Hiring Firm: People Care Health LLP, Thrissur District, Kerala
Work Location: Virtual and based in Boston- USA
Job Description: 
People care health is a healthcare startup based in Thrissur and mentored by researchers in Boston, USA. 
We are looking for a dynamic individual with research and computing skills, especially in AI and data science, to support advanced policy-level implementation research conducted by Dr. Hamad Ibrahim, a medical doctor specializing in the US's medical and public health arena. 
This is an exciting opportunity for young computing students to learn societal challenges and improve their decision-making skills to improve societal growth and development. 
The research engineer/ associate position directly reports to the principal investigator based in Boston, USA. 
High-level candidates for this position would have more significant intellectual curiosity and a passion for creating solutions to solve problems. In addition, we expect candidates to possess integrity, independence, innovative thinking skills, and go-to people who fix problems. 
Primary Duties: 
The right candidate will virtually work directly with the PI in Boston and complete the assignment set by the PI time. 
Robust AI-based computing and data science skills are required to work on this project. 
Awareness of academic research is required to take up this position.
Basic Qualifications
Currently enrolled engineering undergraduate, post graduate, graduate students  and junior faculty are welcome to apply. 
We expect students to have 1-2 years of prior experience in computing, AI, data science, and implementation.
Additions Qualifications
Excellent communication skills: ability to retract and present research findings
Leadership Skills
Product and project management skills.
